I ordered the protein smoothie that had great flavor but was a little sweet. <rate>5</rate>< Review>
Incredibly clean. Great variety of equipment. Never busy, even during peak times (if you‚Äôve been to an Equinox at 6pm, trust that you‚Äôll never have that experience here). Spin classes and CrossFit studios available with pretty regular classes. Facility is split over two levels: downstairs are locker rooms (bring your own lock) with showers, separate two-story CrossFit studio, and a large studio with squat racks and kickboxing bags; upstairs is an open floor with cardio equipment including treadmills, elliptical as, and stair machines (all facing TVs), free weights and benches, and a ton of equipment (yes, even for legs!). Bring your own towel. Friendly staff and plenty of parking, with cafes and markets within 10-50 feet of the entrance, though try an a√ßa√≠ bowl at the bar downstairs. Have been a member for nearly 3 years and I‚Äôm so grateful a facility like this exists in ‚Äúsmall town‚Äù San Luis Obispo. My only wish is that you could scan your membership barcode with an iPhone app instead of a physical tag, but that‚Äôs an incredibly minor caveat.< /Review>

After rescuing a gull with a broken wing from the beach (where we are currently under a high surf warning), we put the bird in a box as instructed by the recording on their message line.  We were in a location of some risk and just packaged the bird, which was showing signs of shock, exhaustion, and likely dehydration, stopping to take no pictures.

We drove over 30 minutes one-way, and after taking one picture on the way inside with the box, we asked the volunteer if we could take a picture of the bird itself.  She was SO nasty!  She said "You were taking pictures out there as I came in!", refuting our statement that we had taken no pictures (argumentative), and followed up with "The time to have done that was when you put it in the box!!".  She did not, I guess, think about the fact that we may have endangered ourselves to save the bird, nor that we had hurried with it to what we thought a safe place, as soon as we possibly could.

I have experience as a Veterinary Tech Assistant, and an incomplete application to volunteer at this center.  I will NEVER assist an organization that keeps staff who hate what they do, and there is no other explanation for how that woman treated us!  Her demeanor and attitude clearly and loudly said that we were not welcome.  One can only hope that she finds *something* to do with herself that makes her a nicer person, lest she , and her affluent free time be all there is in the end.<//Review><pics>None</pics><response>{'time': 1480463797956, 'text': 'Really sorry, Lisa, you had such a bad experience!  I was able to learn which volunteer, not staff member, you saw because she admitted the interaction with you had not gone as well.  My opinion, and it is only that, as I was not there, is that when we have problems at the receiving desk it is usually the result of both parties coming together as strangers at a very emotional moment.  Then it sometimes leads to major misunderstandings, and hurt feelings, precisely because  both parties are both so focused on the animal in question.  I am guessing you were focused on the whole experience of rescuing the bird, and how emotional it all was, and how much you cared about it, and remembering and documenting your success, especially if it was difficult or even scary, and in feeling happy to finally get it to a safe place.  The person receiving the animal is focused on getting that animal back to the veterinarian, or other staff as quickly as possible so care can be given right away. They are trained to be aware of how traumatic any wildlife interaction with humans can be, or if not, how it might contribute to taming that animal, making it vulnerable to humans without your feeling for wildlife, once it is released back to the wild, if it can be.  It might seem to be easy to train people who volunteer at our front desk to be more careful with the people they interact with than the animals, but unfortunately, it is not always that easy with those who are really dedicated to wildlife.  Not sure this possible explanation of how you and the person you saw that day were feeling, and thinking, but I hate to think you retain such a poor opinion of our organization, as we do try awfully hard to do things the best as we can for wildlife, but we are for sure less than perfect. <Rate>3< /Rate>< Text>
Great service and welcoming atmosphere, but probably not the best spot for burritos in town. The flavors that are usually robust in mexican food were minimal in the meats here, and at times the beef had a chewiness the texture of a wet tissue. Great place to stop if you're on the run and want something to hold you over for a few hours that doesnt have to be delicious. Its definitely good enough to eat, but there isn't anything spectacular about it. You'll find that the refried beans and the hot sauce seem to have the most flavor.<//Text>

<name>Denver Dayton< /name><pictures>None<//pictures>< review>
DoD  (Day Old Doughnuts) can't beat them . I don't have much money..., so whenever I can save a little, I do .... so let me start with a short story about this little shop, and the great manager that this shop has. I'm up most nights pretty late , sometimes all night. Late one night , or was it early morning, I was out for some fresh air; I was cold , hungry, and about to fall asleep. So this place is open 24/7 . I had maybe 2,or3 $  . So I order a coffee and I ask if they have any day old doughnuts, you know the ones they are about to throw out ; like they do every day. Well he hooked me up with a small bag ( of doughnuts)to add to my large coffee. Wide awake from the coffee, full belly from the doughnuts I was ready to start my day or continue it anyway. So I always tip them when I can, and sometimes I don't get there early enough for the day old d's , but I am definitely a fan. 5stars and then some.<//review>

< Review>
The deli has moved from their old Eastland Center location to 126 E Shoppers Ln, in Covina just a couple of blocks north. The restaurant space is better but finding a parking space can be a challenge during peak hours. The food is still awesome but it might be my imagination telling me the portion sizes are a bit smaller. Please note that this business recently moved from Workman over to 128 Shoppers Lane (same city). The service here is friendly, the food great, and very reasonably priced The only negative is that if you arrive at noon, good luck finding a parking space.</Review>

<GmapID>0x80c3285294ce9a57:0x58464adc56972ad7</GmapID><username>D L Haddix</username><Review>Please bring another Old World closer to the Inland Empire!</Review><Resp>None<//Resp></record>

<UserId.>106304859915860891916</UserId.><Name>Jennifer Hunker<//Name>< time>
1472842011613< /time>
< rating>
5< /rating>
< Review>
WHAT IT IS
A FULL Italian deli. They stock BOARS HEAD MEATS (!!!), so there's a source of them in West Covina! Get the Everroast Chicken--your taste buds will love you. In addition to the meats, they have various salads and the ubiquitous Italian cookies.

They also have a restaurant section where they serve "Broasted" chicken, sandwiches, pizza, and soups. Please note--it's tucked away on Shopper's Lane, so it can be a little hard to find if you aren't used to the area.

WHAT YOU SHOULD ORDER
Sandwiches, deli meat

AMBIANCE
5 stars
I really like the look of this place. When you enter, you're standing in the deli portion of the store (which is partitioned from the dining room by a shelf). They have the full line of Boar's Head products including their flavored mayonnaise and mustard. The deli counter is to your right--the bar to order food is directly ahead. There's also a little dessert case right next to where you order your food to tempt you.

The dining room is nice and open and features a salad bar--a rarity in this day and age. This location is relatively new and it shows--everything is clean and lovely looking.

FOOD AND DRINKS
5 Stars
I am in love with their chicken salad sandwich. I've never had a chicken salad so good--I usually don't like chicken salad because I hate celery--but they ground everything up so finely that it comes out more like a delicious spread than a chunky salad. They serve that sandwich on a kaiser roll complete with poppy seeds, which just makes the east coaster in me super happy. I've never tried the chicken, but it smells quite good. I've also not tried the pizza.

NICE SURPRISES
Fruit tarts! One of my favorite little dainty desserts, and yet it's so hard to find outside of the Mexican super markets. And they're good, too!

OVERALL
A fantastic little deli for West Covina!< /Review>
